 His childhood was spent in deprivation just like ordinary tribal boys
 unke mata-pita ke liye bacchon ko praathmik shiksha dena bhi ek mushkil kaam tha

 mushkilon bharaa daur16 saal kii umr main ghar kiaarthik sthitisudhaarney ke liye bhajju amarkanta chale gaye

 is naukari se na to khushi mili or na hi aarthik sankat dur hua

 His name quickly spread all around
 gond art main unhen maharath hasil ho gai thi

 agar aap bhi aisa bolne lage hai to samaj len aapako kaam se brake kii jarurat he
 But it is necessary to manage the office as much as it is necessary to take a break correctly
 isliye aap agar chuttee lene ja rahen hai to apanaaen ye 5 tareeke:1
 Information in advance: If you already know about taking leave, then please inform your boss about it
 last time par bataane par aapke program or offis ke kaam donon par asar padataa he
 2
 pehle se nipataae kaam:chuttee par jane se pehle apane jaruri kaam ko nipataaen
 Doing this also reduces the responsibility of the person handling your work and eases you back to work
 3
 Don't forget to check email: If you are in a responsible post and are going on long leave then don't forget to check your mail box
 jaruri mels kaa jawaab dene ke saath reminder tuls kaa istemaal karen
 4
 apana kaam duusare ko saunp kar jaaen:brake lene se pehle apana kaam kisi duusare karmchaaree ko saunp kar jaaen
 Not only this, but well explain your work to another person
 aisa karne se duusare vyakti ko kaam ke dauraan koi dikkat nahin hogi or aapke phone kii ghanti bhi kam bajegi
 5
 tay samay par waapas lauten:aapane bos ko jo samay chuttee kaa bataaya he us tay samay main waapas aaen
 Doing this increases your confidence in the eyes of the boss
